<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of diplomatic missions in Russia</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="415" data-file-width="940" height="177" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg/400px-Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg/600px-Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg/800px-Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg.png 2x" width="400"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Diplomatic_missions_in_the_Russian_Federation.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Map of diplomatic missions in Russia (as of 2012)</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>This is a <b>list of diplomatic missions in Russia</b>. As the world's largest country, a permanent member of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a>, <a href="/wiki/Regional_power" title="Regional power">regional power</a> in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a> and the principal successor state to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_of_Soviet_Socialist_Republics" title="Union of Soviet Socialist Republics">Soviet Union</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian Federation</a> hosts a large diplomatic community in its capital city of <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>. Moscow hosts 148 embassies, with numerous countries maintaining consulates general and consulates throughout the country.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_missions">Other missions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_diplomatic_missions_in_Russia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Other missions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In Moscow</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="900" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_Georgia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Georgia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_Georgia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Georgia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_Georgia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Georgia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/> </span><a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> (Interests Section in Swiss Embassy)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124"><a href="#cite_note-124">[122]</a></sup></li>

<li id="cite_note-92"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-92">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The Consulate-General of Japan was located in <a href="/wiki/Nakhodka" title="Nakhodka">Nakhodka</a> from 1967 until April 1993, when it was relocated to Vladivostok.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-122"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-122">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The Consulate-General of Vietnam was located in <a href="/wiki/Nakhodka" title="Nakhodka">Nakhodka</a> from September 1989 until November 1996, when it was relocated to Vladivostok.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-vietnamvvo_121-1"><a href="#cite_note-vietnamvvo-121">[120]</a></sup></span></li>
</ol>

<th class="navbox-group" scope="row">States with limited<br/>
